       <p>Our good friends at <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.izotope.com/\">iZotope</a> have just announced the next instalment of their award winning software. Commonly referred to as the \"photoshop of the audio world\" - <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.izotope.com/en/products/repair-and-edit/rx-6.html\">RX 6</a> will feature new technologies for post production like mic de-rustle, dialogue isolation, and low-end wind rumble removal.</p>\n                </div>\n              \n\n              \n\n              \n                <!-- Read More
